name:Z‚Äço‚Äçe‚Äçy‚Äçx‚Äçi‚Äçy‚Äçi‚Äçx‚Äçi

posted:Posted April 23, 2024
msg:Landscape context | Facing the highest peak in Guilin

The fog is so thick that it feels like traveling in a painting...
It is a commonplace to say that Guilin's landscape is the best in the world
But only when you are there can you understand that Chinese landscape painting is not abstract, but realistic

Before coming to Guilin, I had already decided to trace some of the best-preserved relics of the Ming and Qing dynasties
Jingjiang Palace and Museum, Sun and Moon Twin Towers, etc.
Of course, the landscape is stunning: Duxiu Peak and Elephant Trunk Hill are also long-awaited
Based on the several hotels I stayed in these days,
If you come to Guilin to play, you can give priority to: Zhengyang Pedestrian Street/Dongxixiang Business District

This trip is recommended: [Boyin Yi Nianjian] Hotel
There are mainly three reasons: good location + good aesthetics + good service

First of all, the good location is that it is located in the most prosperous business district in Guilin-Dongxixiang
You can see Jingjiang Palace & Duxiu Peak without leaving the hotel. When staying here, you can walk directly to the hotel in a few minutes
Save the road and greatly improve the travel experience

Good aesthetics is reflected in the overall environment of antique and modern integration
The overall room furnishings are bookish, ancient, calm, and the space is open and a**ospheric
At the same time, the room configuration is also very intelligent, very clever and attentive to integrate two points
Green plants and flowers are also integrated into the stay experience

The good service is mainly to tie my heart with delicious food
In short, the breakfast is really delicious! I would like to call it the top rice noodles in Guilin
After a short sleep in the morning, the breakfast that combines Chinese and Western cuisines completely awakened my good mood
In addition, the front desk has airport pick-up/high-speed rail pick-up services after reservation, and it is also very convenient for smart robots to help pick up takeout

One thought reveals the cultural context and one thought knows the mountains and rivers
The green mountains are far away and the nearby water is smoky
The perfect experience of this Guilin trip starts here~

We booked a twin room, the room is more than 30 square meters, clean, tidy, details are in place, there is a capsule coffee machine, welcome fruit. When checking in in the afternoon, there is afternoon tea in the lobby, which is quite rich in content. I like lychee tremella soup, which is light and sweet and moist, very comfortable.
The twin beds in the room are definitely the highlight, with a width of 1.5 meters. It is very practical to bring a baby out. The mattress is also comfortable. It has a moderate soft drink and a good support. The quilts have also been replaced with summer quilts. I really like it. The quality of the toiletries is also very good!
The staff are polite, kind, and have a good attitude. It should be said that they are responsive. There was an aunt at breakfast who was very kind. She offered to tell us that we could order freshly made Guilin rice noodles first, and served them herself. I didn‚Äôt see fried eggs on the dining table. After I ordered them, she brought them over immediately. It‚Äôs really heartwarming, thank you!
The only regret is that the exterior view of the room is a bit bad. Outside the window, it should be the roof of the building next door. The tiles are flying around and it is very messy, which affects the experience of staying. We simply closed the curtains. In addition, there is a small swimming pool on the top floor, about 4m*4m in size. The picture promotion is a bit distorted, like a large infinity pool.
